		<script type="text/javascript">

		    // Grab the current date
		    var currentDate = new Date();

		    // Set some date in the future. In this case, it's always Jan 1
		    //var futureDate = new Date("July 08, 2016 23:59:00");

		    var futureDate = new Date("Fri Aug 03 2016 07:00:00");

		    // Calculate the difference in seconds between the future and current date
		    var diff = futureDate.getTime() / 1000 - currentDate.getTime() / 1000;

		    /*Added By Kenny Sekhwela
                For Count Down timer for Special Votes*/

		    var myShowCountDowntoOpen = new Date("Thu Jun 09 2016 21:00:00"); //Show CountDown to open date
		    var myShowCountDowntoEnd = new Date("Thu Jun 09 2016 23:59:59"); //Close Countdown to open date
		   
		    if (currentDate > myShowCountDowntoOpen && currentDate < myShowCountDowntoEnd) {
		      
	           
		            //document.getElementById("ctl00_ctl00_uxContentBody_uxContentBody_uxSpecialVoteCountDown").style.display = "inline";
		            // Calculate the difference in seconds between the future and current date
		            diff = myShowCountDowntoEnd.getTime() / 1000 - currentDate.getTime() / 1000;
		            //document.getElementById("ctl00_ctl00_uxContentBody_uxContentBody_uxSpecialVoteCountDownHeader").innerText = 'until Special Vote application open';
		            //document.getElementById("ctl00_ctl00_uxContentBody_uxContentBody_uxSpecialVoteCountDownHeader").style.color = "#DF8C74";

		    }
		    else {
		        if (currentDate > myShowCountDowntoEnd && currentDate < futureDate) {
		          
		            //document.getElementById("ctl00_ctl00_uxContentBody_uxContentBody_uxSpecialVoteCountDown").style.display = "inline";
		            diff = futureDate.getTime() / 1000 - currentDate.getTime() / 1000;

		            if (diff < 0) { diff = 0;}
		            //document.getElementById("ctl00_ctl00_uxContentBody_uxContentBody_uxSpecialVoteCountDownHeader").innerText = 'until Special Vote application close';
		            //document.getElementById("ctl00_ctl00_uxContentBody_uxContentBody_uxSpecialVoteCountDownHeader").style.color = "#fff";

		        }
		    }

		    var preloader = ($.browser.msie) ? false : true;

		    $(document).ready(function () {
		        var options = {
		            autoPlay: true,
		            autoPlayDelay: 10000,
		            nextButton: true,
		            prevButton: true,
		            preloader: preloader,
		            animateStartingFrameIn: true,
		            transitionThreshold: 500,
		            fallback: {
		                theme: "slide",
		                speed: 1000
		            }
		        };

		        var sequence = $("#sequence").sequence(options).data("sequence");

		        sequence.afterLoaded = function () {
		            $(".info").css('display', 'block');
		            $("#sequence").hover(
					        function () {
					            $(".prev, .next").stop().animate({ opacity: 0.7 }, 300);
					        },
					        function () {
					            $(".prev, .next").stop().animate({ opacity: 0 }, 300);
					        }
					);

		            $(".prev, .next").hover(
					        function () {
					            $(this).stop().animate({ opacity: 1 }, 200);
					        },
					        function () {
					            $(this).stop().animate({ opacity: 0.7 }, 200);
					        }
					);
		        }
